    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer568485068748724384">Set in the 1940's, Rivers Never Fill The Sea follows the lives of two families; the Masons and the Brennans. Mike Mason is a rapacious land developer in the coastal town of Woodrose, California. Hostility begins when Mason buys out a home belonging to former boxer, Ty Brennan, forcing the eviction of his family. The animosity between the two of them grows further when Ty's</span>
  <span id="freeText568485068748724384" style="display:none">Set in the 1940's, Rivers Never Fill The Sea follows the lives of two families; the Masons and the Brennans. Mike Mason is a rapacious land developer in the coastal town of Woodrose, California. Hostility begins when Mason buys out a home belonging to former boxer, Ty Brennan, forcing the eviction of his family. The animosity between the two of them grows further when Ty's son and Mike's daughter fall in love, complicating matters. A gambling ship off shore, a dangerous and covert operation that carries a heavy consequence, and a devastating cyclone all come together one fateful summer and nothing would ever be the same.</span>

<div id="review_2305272550" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2305272550" />
    <a title="Debra Walter" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/78136984-debra-walter"><img alt="Debra Walter" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1519347449p2/78136984.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2305272550?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra Walter" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra Walter" href="/user/show/78136984-debra-walter">Debra Walter</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/38894748-rivers-never-fill-the-sea">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2305272550" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10536139174962862563">This was an absorbing read. The descriptions of nature are almost poetic and I loved every character. I would've liked to know more about some of the character's individual lives. I wanted to know more about why Ty Brennan ended up such a mean person? What his back story was? And Kate's parents could have a story all of their own! But at 400 pages I think the author did a great job of giving the reader just enough. Overall, a beautifully written novel that just flows so easily.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText11210127560888365276" style="display:none">Wow, well, what to tackle first. The book reads beautifully with lots of skillfully written descriptions and it really puts you there. The storyline is interesting and takes you from beginning to a glimpse of conclusion to beginning again. Sounds complicated but it's flows very easily and you don't get lost. There's a plethora of things going on; romance, rivalry, familial discord, and it tackles a lot of subjects so there's never a dull moment. From the first page to the last, it was a hard book to put down and I would pick it up at various times of the day whenever I got the chance. In conclusion, don't miss out and read this one. Look forward to more from this writer.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1104473143815788713">Wish I could have given this book 5 stars since the only thing I believe it lacked was that I would have liked for the author to expand more on my favorite characters. In conclusion, I think this story should have been longer so that the reader could indulge in the different lives of the characters.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('I81Sx9ZMscRiMR05B3SsU5p32JXEpA3Y3obHNykf8L9XoFbWrDaS4SaAHuX06oH1Bg8Lt7p7cd5umbcHYeYE1A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('A3a3lNoNnMBlwGZc4xKus68IBLMG5Byq3S9jG3fJB5h3G7OFoHe/5SFxZYAQjIMVM3DXkXg7YKxtMBMrPzDz8w==')})
  }
//]]>
